@param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n126:    * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n127:    * @param strike the FX strike\n128:    * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n129:    * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n130:    * @param paymentDateAdjustment the adjustment to apply to the payment date\n131:    * @return an equivalent fx vanilla option\n132:    */\n133:   public static FxVanillaOption of(\n134:       LongShort longShort,\n135:       ZonedDateTime expiry,\n136:       CurrencyPair currencyPair,\n137:       PutCall putCall,\n138:       double strike,\n139:       double baseNotional,\n140:       LocalDate paymentDate,\n141:       BusinessDayAdjustment paymentDateAdjustment) {\n142: \n143:     ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n144:     ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n145: \n146:     // for a vanilla call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n147:     // for a vanilla put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n148:     double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n149:     double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n150:     double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n151:     CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getBase(), baseAmount);\n152:     CurrencyAmount counterCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getCounter(), counterAmount);\n153:     FxSingle equivalentUnderlying = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n154:         FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate) :\n155:         FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate, paymentDateAdjustment);\n156: \n157:     return FxVanillaOption.builder()\n158:         .longShort(longShort)\n159:         .expiryDate(expiry.toLocalDate())\n160:         .expiryTime(expiry.toLocalTime())\n161:         .expiryZone(expiry.getZone())\n162:         .underlying(equivalentUnderlying)\n163:         .build();\n164:   }\n165: \n166:   //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n167:   @ImmutableValidator\n168: The\n * option is European, exercised only on the exercise date.\n * <p>\n * For example, a call on a 'EUR 1.00 / USD -1.41' exchange is the option to perform a foreign exchange on the expiry\n * date, where USD 1.41 is paid to receive EUR 1.00.\n */\n@BeanDefinition\npublic final class FxEuropeanOption\n    implements FxOptionProduct, Resolvable<ResolvedFxEuropeanOption>, ImmutableBean, Serializable {\n\n  /**\n   * Whether the option is long or short.\n   * <p>\n   * At expiry, the long party will have the option to enter in this transaction; the short party will, at the option of\n   * the long party, potentially enter into the inverse transaction.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final LongShort longShort;\n  /**\n   * The expiry date of the option.\n   * <p>\n   * The option is European, and can only be exercised on the expiry date.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final LocalDate expiryDate;\n  /**\n   * The expiry time of the option.\n   * <p>\n   * The expiry time is related to the expiry date and time-zone.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final LocalTime expiryTime;\n  /**\n   * The time-zone of the expiry time.\n   * <p>\n   * The expiry time-zone is related to the expiry date and time.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final ZoneId expiryZone;\n  /**\n   * The underlying foreign exchange transaction.\n   * <p>\n   * At expiry, if the option is in the money, this foreign exchange will occur.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final FxSingle underlying;\n\n  /**\n   * Creates an equivalent {@code FxEuropeanOption} using currency pair, option expiry, call/put flag, strike, base\n   * currency notional, and underlying payment date.\n   * <p>\n   * No payment date adjustments apply.\n   *\n   * @param longShort the long/short flag of the option\n   * @param expiry the option expiry\n   * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n   * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n   * @param strike the FX strike\n   * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @return an equivalent fx european option\n   */\n  public static FxEuropeanOption of(\n      LongShort longShort,\n      ZonedDateTime expiry,\n      CurrencyPair currencyPair,\n      PutCall putCall,\n      double strike,\n      double baseNotional,\n      LocalDate paymentDate) {\n\n    return of(longShort, expiry, currencyPair, putCall, strike, baseNotional, paymentDate, null);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Creates an equivalent {@code FxEuropeanOption} using currency pair, option expiry, call/put flag, strike, base\n   * currency notional, underlying payment date, and payment date adjustment.\n   *\n   * @param longShort the long/short flag of the option\n   * @param expiry the option expiry\n   * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n   * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n   * @param strike the FX strike\n   * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @param paymentDateAdjustment the adjustment to apply to the payment date\n   * @return an equivalent fx european option\n   */\n  public static FxEuropeanOption of(\n      LongShort longShort,\n      ZonedDateTime expiry,\n      CurrencyPair currencyPair,\n      PutCall putCall,\n      double strike,\n      double baseNotional,\n      LocalDate paymentDate,\n      BusinessDayAdjustment paymentDateAdjustment) {\n\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n\n    // for a european call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n    // for a european put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n    double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n    double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n    double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n    CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getBase(), baseAmount);\n    CurrencyAmount counterCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getCounter(), counterAmount);\n    FxSingle equivalentUnderlying = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate) :\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate, paymentDateAdjustment);\n\n    return FxEuropeanOption.builder()\n        .longShort(longShort)\n        .expiryDate(expiry.toLocalDate())\n        .expiryTime(expiry.toLocalTime())\n        .expiryZone(expiry.getZone())\n        .underlying(equivalentUnderlying)\n        .build();\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @ImmutableValidator\n  private void validate() {\n    inOrderOrEqual(expiryDate, underlying.getPaymentDate(), \"expiryDate\", \"underlying.paymentDate\");\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n  /**\n   * Gets currency pair of the base currency and counter currency.\n   * <p>\n   * This currency pair is conventional, thus indifferent to the direction of FX.\n   *\n   * @return the currency pair\n   */\n  @Override\n  public CurrencyPair getCurrencyPair() {\n    return underlying.getCurrencyPair();\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Gets the expiry date-time.\n   * <p>\n   * The option expires at this date and time.\n   * <p>\n   * The result is returned by combining the expiry date, time and time-zone.\n   *\n   * @return the expiry date and time\n   */\n  @Override\n  public ZonedDateTime getExpiry() {\n    return expiryDate.atTime(expiryTime).atZone(expiryZone);\n  }\n\n option\n   * @param expiry the option expiry\n   * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n   * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n   * @param strike the FX strike\n   * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @param paymentDateAdjustment the adjustment to apply to the payment date\n   * @return an equivalent fx european option\n   */\n  public static FxEuropeanOption of(\n      LongShort longShort,\n      ZonedDateTime expiry,\n      CurrencyPair ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n\n    // for a european call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n    // for a european put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n    double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n    double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n    double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n    CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate) :\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate, paymentDateAdjustment);\n\n    return FxEuropeanOption.builder()\n        .longShort(longShort)\n        .expiryDate(expiry.toLocalDate())\n        .expiryTime(expiry.toLocalTime())\n        .expiryZone(expiry.getZone())\n        .underlying(equivalentUnderlying)\n        .build();\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n
